Flink-specific than Kafka's Deserializer, supports Collector-based output\\n   - Implements interface (defines)\\n\\n### Kafka-Flink Integration Example\\n\\nThe Flink codebase includes an example implementation:\\n\\n1. **EventDeSerializationSchema** implements DeserializationSchema<Event>, SerializationSchema<Event>`\\n   - Implements Flink's `DeserializationSchema` interface\\n   - Shows how to integrate with Kafka in Flink by wrapping both Flink's DeserializationSchema and SerializationSchema\\n   - Used in StateMachineExample with `KafkaSource` via `KafkaRecordDeserializationSchema.valueOnly(new EventDeSerializationSchema())`\\n\\n### Integration Pattern\\n\\nThe serialization boundary between Kafka and Flink is bridged through:\\n- Kafka's `Deserializer<T>` interface (low-level, topic-aware)\\n- Flink's `DeserializationSchema<T>` interface (high-level, Flink-integrated with metrics and collector support)\\n- The Flink Kafka connector provides adapter classes like `KafkaRecordDeserializationSchema` that wrap Flink's `DeserializationSchema` for use with Kafka sources\\n\\nThis two-layer abstraction allows Flink to maintain its own serialization semantics while seamlessly integrating with Kafka's serialization framework.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
